### [264] [Epistemic Observability in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20531)
*Tony Mason*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 模型在编造内容时报告最高置信度，文本监督存在根本性限制，通过导出计算副产品（如逐词熵）可突破该限制，为系统构建者提供验证资源分配决策依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究发现模型在编造内容时反而报告最高置信度，这揭示了文本监督的根本局限性：仅通过输出文本无法可靠区分真实回答与合理编造，需要新的监控方法。

Method: 1) 实证分析四个模型家族（OLMo-3、Llama-3.1、Qwen3、Mistral）的置信度-准确性关系；2) 形式化证明文本监督的不可可能性；3) 构建张量接口导出计算副产品（逐词熵和log概率分布）；4) 建立验证预算与检测准确性的成本曲面。

Result: 1) 模型置信度与准确性呈负相关（AUC 0.28-0.36，0.5为随机猜测）；2) 逐词熵达到池化AUC 0.757，比所有文本基线高2.5-3.9个百分点；3) 熵信号在不同架构间具有良好泛化性（Spearman ρ=0.762）。

Conclusion: 文本监督存在根本性限制，无法可靠检测模型编造；通过导出计算副产品（特别是逐词熵）可显著提升检测性能；为系统构建者提供了实用的验证资源分配决策框架。

Abstract: We find that models report highest confidence precisely when they are fabricating. Across four model families (OLMo-3, Llama-3.1, Qwen3, Mistral), self-reported confidence inversely correlates with accuracy, with AUC ranging from 0.28 to 0.36 where 0.5 is random guessing.
  We prove, under explicit formal assumptions, that this is not a capability gap but an observational one. Under text-only observation, where a supervisor sees only the model's output text, no monitoring system can reliably distinguish honest model outputs from plausible fabrications. We prove two results: first, that any policy conditioning only on the query cannot satisfy epistemic honesty across ambiguous world states; second, that no learning algorithm optimizing reward from a text-only supervisor can converge to honest behavior when the supervisor's observations are identical for both grounded and fabricated responses. Within our formal model, these impossibilities hold regardless of model scale or training procedure, including RLHF and instruction tuning.
  We construct a tensor interface that escapes the impossibility by exporting computational byproducts (per-token entropy and log-probability distributions) that are structurally coupled to correctness under standard training. Per-token entropy achieves pooled AUC 0.757, outperforming all text baselines by 2.5--3.9 percentage points at every budget level tested (10\%, 20\%, 30\%). The entropy signal generalizes across architectures (Spearman $ρ= 0.762$).
  The core contribution is a cost surface where the empirical mapping from verification budget (fraction of queries receiving expensive checks) to detection accuracy for each judge strategy is a practical lookup for system builders deciding how to allocate verification resources. The contribution is the map. The territory is the system you are building.

</details>


### [265] [Incremental GNN Embedding Computation on Streaming Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20622)
*Qiange Wang,Haoran Lv,Yanfeng Zhang,Weng-Fai Wong,Bingsheng He*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出了一种用于流图GNN推理的高效增量计算框架，通过算子解耦和重排序将全邻居计算转换为受影响子图计算，显著减少冗余计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流图GNN推理依赖运行时嵌入计算(RTEC)来捕获图变化，但该过程涉及繁重的多跳图遍历开销，计算效率低下。观察到图演化过程中大部分中间结果保持不变，可以通过增量方法有效消除冗余计算。

Method: 1) 将GNN计算解耦为一组通用的细粒度算子并安全重排序，将昂贵的全邻居GNN计算转换为对受影响子图的高效计算形式；2) 为处理大规模历史结果，开发GPU-CPU协同处理系统，通过通信优化调度将嵌入卸载到CPU内存。

Result: 在不同图规模和GNN模型上的实验表明，该方法减少64%-99%的计算量，相比现有解决方案获得1.7x-145.8x的加速比。

Conclusion: 提出的增量RTEC框架在保持原始全邻居计算语义和精度的同时，显著提升了流图GNN推理的计算效率，支持具有复杂消息传递模式的各种GNN模型。

Abstract: Graph Neural Network (GNN) on streaming graphs has gained increasing popularity. However, its practical deployment remains challenging, as the inference process relies on Runtime Embedding Computation (RTEC) to capture recent graph changes. This process incurs heavyweight multi-hop graph traversal overhead, which significantly undermines computation efficiency. We observe that the intermediate results for large portions of the graph remain unchanged during graph evolution, and thus redundant computations can be effectively eliminated through carefully designed incremental methods. In this work, we propose an efficient framework for incrementalizing RTEC on streaming graphs.The key idea is to decouple GNN computation into a set of generalized, fine-grained operators and safely reorder them, transforming the expensive full-neighbor GNN computation into a more efficient form over the affected subgraph. With this design, our framework preserves the semantics and accuracy of the original full-neighbor computation while supporting a wide range of GNN models with complex message-passing patterns. To further scale to graphs with massive historical results, we develop a GPU-CPU co-processing system that offloads embeddings to CPU memory with communication-optimized scheduling. Experiments across diverse graph sizes and GNN models show that our method reduces computation by 64%-99% and achieves 1.7x-145.8x speedups over existing solutions.

</details>


### [266] [Modernizing Amdahl's Law: How AI Scaling Laws Shape Computer Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20654)
*Chien-Ping Lu*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 论文重新表述阿姆达尔定律，适用于现代异构系统和可扩展工作负载，揭示了有限崩溃阈值：超过临界可扩展比例时，专业化变得次优，最优专用硬件投资降为零，形成相变而非渐近尾部。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典阿姆达尔定律假设串行与并行工作的固定分解和同质复制，而现代系统结合了专用加速器、可编程计算、张量数据通路和演化流水线。核心矛盾不仅是串行与并行分割，还包括异构硬件间的资源分配、效率差异以及决定额外计算如何有效转化为价值的工作负载结构。

Method: 重新表述阿姆达尔定律以适用于现代异构系统和可扩展工作负载，分析得出有限崩溃阈值。当可扩展比例超过临界值时，即使专用硬件效率优势存在，专业化也变得次优，最优专用投资降为零。

Result: 分析揭示了相变现象而非渐近尾部：超过临界可扩展分数后，专业化变得次优，最优专用硬件投资降为零。这一框架解释了GPU可编程性增加的原因以及为何领域专用AI加速器未能取代GPU。

Conclusion: 现代异构系统的性能界限不仅取决于串行与并行分割，还受资源分配、硬件效率差异和工作负载结构影响。有限崩溃阈值表明，当可扩展比例足够高时，专业化策略失效，这解释了GPU持续主导地位和领域专用加速器的局限性。

Abstract: Classical Amdahl's Law assumes a fixed decomposition between serial and parallel work and homogeneous replication; historically, it bounds how much parallel speedup is attainable. Modern systems instead combine specialized accelerators with programmable compute, tensor datapaths, and evolving pipelines, while empirical scaling laws shift which stages absorb marginal compute. The central tension is therefore not the serial-versus-parallel split alone, but resource allocation across heterogeneous hardware, given efficiency differences, and workload structures that determine how effectively additional compute can be converted into value. We reformulate Amdahl's Law for modern heterogeneous systems with scalable workloads. The analysis yields a finite collapse threshold: beyond a critical scalable fraction, specialization becomes suboptimal for any efficiency advantage of specialized hardware over programmable compute, and optimal specialized investment falls to zero, a phase transition rather than an asymptotic tail. We use this framework to interpret increasing GPU programmability and why domain-specific AI accelerators have not displaced GPUs.

</details>


### [267] [Compass: Optimizing Compound AI Workflows for Dynamic Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20821)
*Milos Gravara,Juan Luis Herrera,Stefan Nastic*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: Compass框架通过离线优化和在线自适应实现复合AI系统的动态配置切换，在固定基础设施下平衡精度、延迟和成本目标


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复合AI系统需要在固定基础设施上满足精度、延迟和成本目标，但现有方法仅优化精度且不考虑负载变化。系统可以通过配置切换在基础设施容量内权衡精度和延迟

Method: Compass框架包含三个组件：COMPASS-V算法使用有限差分引导搜索和爬山-横向扩展组合发现精度可行的配置；Planner在目标硬件上分析配置并使用排队论模型推导切换策略；Elastico控制器监控队列深度并根据阈值切换配置

Result: COMPASS-V在保持100%召回率的同时，相比穷举搜索平均减少57.5%的配置评估，在严格精度阈值下效率提升达95.3%。运行时自适应在动态负载模式下实现90-98%的SLO合规性，比静态高精度基线提高71.6%，同时比静态快速基线提高3-5%的精度

Conclusion: Compass框架通过动态配置切换有效解决了复合AI系统在固定基础设施下的精度-延迟权衡问题，实现了在动态负载条件下的高效自适应

Abstract: Compound AI is a distributed intelligence approach that represents a unified system orchestrating specialized AI/ML models with engineered software components into AI workflows. Compound AI production deployments must satisfy accuracy, latency, and cost objectives under varying loads. However, many deployments operate on fixed infrastructure where horizontal scaling is not viable. Existing approaches optimize solely for accuracy and do not consider changes in workload conditions. We observe that compound AI systems can switch between configurations to fit infrastructure capacity, trading accuracy for latency based on current load. This requires discovering multiple Pareto-optimal configurations from a combinatorial search space and determining when to switch between them at runtime. We present Compass, a novel framework that enables dynamic configuration switching through offline optimization and online adaptation. Compass consists of three components: COMPASS-V algorithm for configuration discovery, Planner for switching policy derivation, and Elastico Controller for runtime adaptation. COMPASS-V discovers accuracy-feasible configurations using finite-difference guided search and a combination of hill-climbing and lateral expansion. Planner profiles these configurations on target hardware and derives switching policies using a queuing theory based model. Elastico monitors queue depth and switches configurations based on derived thresholds. Across two compound AI workflows, COMPASS-V achieves 100% recall while reducing configuration evaluations by 57.5% on average compared to exhaustive search, with efficiency gains reaching 95.3% at tight accuracy thresholds. Runtime adaptation achieves 90-98% SLO compliance under dynamic load patterns, improving SLO compliance by 71.6% over static high-accuracy baselines, while simultaneously improving accuracy by 3-5% over static fast baselines.

</details>


### [268] [Communication Lower Bounds and Algorithms for Sketching with Random Dense Matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20966)
*Hussam Al Daas,Grey Ballard,Laura Grigori,Md Taufique Hussain,Suraj Kumar,Mohammad Marufur Rahman,Kathryn Rouse*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 该论文研究了分布式内存环境中矩阵素描（sketching）的通信下界，提出了通信最优算法，并扩展到Nyström近似计算，在CPU和GPU超级计算系统上验证了并行可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 矩阵素描在随机线性代数和机器学习中广泛应用，但在分布式内存环境中，通信开销成为现代超级计算集群的关键瓶颈。尽管重要性日益增长，但分布式内存并行素描策略尚未得到充分探索。

Method: 1. 建立使用稠密矩阵进行素描的通信下界，确定并行执行所需的最小数据移动量；2. 提出通信最优算法证明下界紧性；3. 扩展方法确定Nyström近似计算的通信下界；4. 设计通信成本接近下界的新型并行算法；5. 在现代CPU和GPU超级计算基础设施上实现算法。

Result: 1. 证明了素描的通信下界，发现少量处理器时无需通信；2. 提出的算法通信成本达到下界，证明下界紧性；3. 成功扩展到Nyström近似计算；4. 算法在现代超级计算系统上展示了良好的并行可扩展性。

Conclusion: 该工作填补了分布式内存并行素描策略的研究空白，建立了通信下界并提出了通信最优算法，为大规模矩阵素描在超级计算环境中的高效实现提供了理论基础和实用方案。

Abstract: Sketching is widely used in randomized linear algebra for low-rank matrix approximation, column subset selection, and many other problems, and it has gained significant traction in machine learning applications. However, sketching large matrices often necessitates distributed memory algorithms, where communication overhead becomes a critical bottleneck on modern supercomputing clusters. Despite its growing relevance, distributed-memory parallel strategies for sketching remain largely unexplored. In this work, we establish communication lower bounds for sketching using dense matrices that determine how much data movement is required to perform it in parallel. One important observation of our lower bounds is that no communication is required for a small number of processors. We show that our lower bounds are tight by presenting communication optimal algorithms. Furthermore, we extend our approach to determine communication lower bounds for computations of Nyström approximation where sketching is applied twice. We also introduce novel parallel algorithms whose communication costs are close to the lower bounds. Finally, we implement our algorithms on modern state-of-the-art supercomputing infrastructures which have both CPU- and GPU-equipped systems and demonstrate their parallel scalability.

</details>


### [269] [NeSy-Edge: Neuro-Symbolic Trustworthy Self-Healing in the Computing Continuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21145)
*Peihan Ye,Alfreds Lapkovskis,Alaa Saleh,Qiyang Zhang,Praveen Kumar Donta*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: NeSy-Edge：一种用于计算连续体中可信自愈的神经符号框架，采用边缘优先设计，在资源受限的边缘节点进行本地感知和推理，仅在最终诊断阶段调用云模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代AI服务的计算需求正从集中式云向边缘和终端设备扩展，但这些环境的规模、异构性和跨层依赖使得弹性难以维持。现有故障管理方法通常过于静态、碎片化或繁重，无法支持及时的自愈，特别是在噪声日志和边缘资源约束下。

Method: NeSy-Edge将原始运行时日志转换为结构化事件表示，构建先验约束的稀疏符号因果图，并将因果证据与历史故障排除知识集成，用于根因分析和恢复建议。采用边缘优先设计，资源受限的边缘节点执行本地感知和推理，云模型仅在最终诊断阶段被调用。

Result: 在具有多个语义噪声级别的代表性Loghub数据集上评估，即使在最高噪声水平下，NeSy-Edge仍保持鲁棒性，实现高达75%的根因分析准确率和65%的端到端准确率，同时在约1500MB本地内存内运行。

Conclusion: NeSy-Edge为计算连续体中的可信自愈提供了一个有效的神经符号框架，通过边缘优先设计和因果推理集成，在资源受限环境下实现了鲁棒的故障诊断和恢复能力。

Abstract: The computational demands of modern AI services are increasingly shifting execution beyond centralized clouds toward a computing continuum spanning edge and end devices. However, the scale, heterogeneity, and cross-layer dependencies of these environments make resilience difficult to maintain. Existing fault-management methods are often too static, fragmented, or heavy to support timely self-healing, especially under noisy logs and edge resource constraints. To address these limitations, this paper presents NeSy-Edge, a neuro-symbolic framework for trustworthy self-healing in the computing continuum. The framework follows an edge-first design, where a resource-constrained edge node performs local perception and reasoning, while a cloud model is invoked only at the final diagnosis stage. Specifically, NeSy-Edge converts raw runtime logs into structured event representations, builds a prior-constrained sparse symbolic causal graph, and integrates causal evidence with historical troubleshooting knowledge for root-cause analysis and recovery recommendation. We evaluate our work on representative Loghub datasets under multiple levels of semantic noise, considering parsing quality, causal reasoning, end-to-end diagnosis, and edge-side resource usage. The results show that NeSy-Edge remains robust even at the highest noise level, achieving up to 75% root-cause analysis accuracy and 65% end-to-end accuracy while operating within about 1500 MB of local memory.

</details>


### [270] [Decidability of Livelock Detection for Parameterized Self-Disabling Unidirectional Rings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21443)
*Aly Farahat*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 该论文证明了对于参数化对称单向环中具有有界域ℤₘ的自禁用进程，活锁检测在多项式时间内是可判定的。算法运行时间为O(|T|³)，独立于环大小K。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究参数化对称单向环系统中的活锁检测问题，旨在为这类系统提供高效的活锁检测算法，解决Farahat代数特征化中未解决的判定性问题。

Method: 基于Farahat的代数特征化，设计多项式时间算法：计算转换集T上紧缩单调算子的最大不动点。算法独立于环大小K，通过检查不动点是否为空来判断活锁存在性。

Result: 证明了活锁检测在多项式时间内可判定，算法复杂度为O(|T|³)。算法还能处理(1,1)-非对称情况，其中一个特殊进程P₀与其他K-1个相同进程不同。

Conclusion: 该工作为参数化对称单向环系统提供了高效的活锁检测算法，基于代数特征化实现了多项式时间判定，解决了先前工作中未解决的判定性问题。

Abstract: We prove that livelock detection is \emph{decidable in polynomial time} for parameterized symmetric unidirectional rings of self-disabling processes with bounded domain $\mathbb{Z}_m$. Given a protocol specified by its set of local transitions $T$, the algorithm decides whether a livelock exists for \emph{some} ring size $K\!\geq\!2$, running in $O(|T|^3)$ time independent of $K$. The algorithm computes the greatest fixed point of a deflationary monotone operator on the finite set $T$ and returns \emph{livelock} iff the fixed point is non-empty. The livelock freedom argument rests on maximality: the fix-point is the largest set of transitions that can together sustain a pseudolivelock at every process; its emptiness certifies freedom for all $K$ without any search over ring sizes. The work is grounded in the algebraic characterization of livelocks from Farahat~\citep{farahat2012}, which establishes necessary and sufficient conditions for livelock existence but does not address decidability. We also handle the $(1,1)$-asymmetric case in which one distinguished process $P_0$ differs from the remaining $K\!-\!1$ identical processes. Code and algebraic foundation are at the URL: https://github.com/cosmoparadox/mathematical-tools.

</details>


### [271] [Communication-Avoiding SpGEMM via Trident Partitioning on Hierarchical GPU Interconnects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21444)
*Julian Bellavita,Lorenzo Pichetti,Thomas Pasquali,Flavio Vella,Giulia Guidi*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: Trident是一种层次感知的2D分布式稀疏矩阵乘法算法，通过通信避免技术和异步通信利用现代超级计算机的层次化异构互连架构，显著减少节点间通信并提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀疏矩阵乘法(SpGEMM)是科学计算和大规模数据分析的关键内核，但非结构化稀疏性限制了内存效率和可扩展性。在分布式内存中，跨节点交换和合并部分乘积的成本进一步制约性能。现代异构超级计算机具有深度层次化的GPU互连，现有SpGEMM实现忽视了节点内与节点间带宽差异，导致不必要的数据移动和同步，未能充分利用快速的节点内互连。

Method: 提出Trident算法，采用层次感知的2D分布式SpGEMM方法。核心是新颖的三叉戟分区方案，通过通信避免技术和异步通信，利用节点内GPU间高于节点间带宽的优势，实现层次感知分解并减少节点间通信。

Result: 在非结构化矩阵上，Trident相比2D SpGEMM实现了最高2.38倍加速，几何平均加速为1.54倍。在NERSC的Perlmutter超级计算机上，将节点间通信量减少高达2倍。在马尔可夫聚类应用中，相比竞争策略实现了最高2倍加速。

Conclusion: Trident通过层次感知的2D分布式SpGEMM算法有效解决了现代异构超级计算机上的稀疏矩阵乘法性能瓶颈，显著减少了节点间通信并提升了整体性能，在真实应用中表现出优越性。

Abstract: The multiplication of two sparse matrices, known as SpGEMM, is a key kernel in scientific computing and large-scale data analytics, underpinning graph algorithms, machine learning, simulations, and computational biology, where sparsity is often highly unstructured. The unstructured sparsity makes achieving high performance challenging because it limits both memory efficiency and scalability. In distributed memory, the cost of exchanging and merging partial products across nodes further constrains performance. These issues are exacerbated on modern heterogeneous supercomputers with deep, hierarchical GPU interconnects. Current SpGEMM implementations overlook the gap between intra-node and inter-node bandwidth, resulting in unnecessary data movement and synchronization not fully exploiting the fast intra-node interconnect. To address these challenges, we introduce Trident, a hierarchy-aware 2D distributed SpGEMM algorithm that uses communication-avoiding techniques and asynchronous communication to exploit the hierarchical and heterogeneous architecture of modern supercomputing interconnect. Central to Trident is the novel trident partitioning scheme, which enables hierarchy-aware decomposition and reduces internode communication by leveraging the higher bandwidth between GPUs within a node compared to across nodes. Here, we evaluate Trident on unstructured matrices, achieving up to $2.38\times$ speedup over a 2D SpGEMM with a corresponding geometric mean speedup of $1.54\times$. Trident reduces internode communication volume by up to $2\times$ on NERSC's Perlmutter supercomputer. Furthermore, we demonstrate the effectiveness of Trident in speeding up Markov Clustering, achieving up to $2\times$ speedup compared to competing strategies.

</details>


### [272] [exaCB: Reproducible Continuous Benchmark Collections at Scale Leveraging an Incremental Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22251)
*Jayesh Badwaik,Mathis Bode,Michal Rajski,Andreas Herten*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: exaCB框架为JUPITER百亿亿次系统提供持续基准测试，将基准测试集成到CI/CD工作流中，支持大规模应用性能评估和回归检测


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高性能计算系统异构性增加和向百亿亿次架构转型，需要跨多样化工作负载进行系统化、可重复的性能评估。虽然持续集成确保软件工程功能正确性，但HPC性能和能效评估通常在CI工作流之外进行，这促使需要持续基准测试作为补充方法

Method: 开发exaCB框架，通过可重用CI/CD组件、已建立的测试工具和共享报告协议，支持应用团队将基准测试集成到工作流中。框架支持渐进式采用，允许基准测试从基本可运行性逐步发展到更高级的仪器化和可重复性

Result: 在JUPITER早期访问计划JUREAP中，exaCB实现了对70多个不同成熟度应用的持续基准测试，支持跨应用分析、性能跟踪和能源感知研究。展示了在大型多样化科学应用集合上进行持续基准测试的实用性

Conclusion: exaCB框架为百亿亿次HPC系统提供了一种实用的持续基准测试方法，支持大规模、系统级研究，通过将基准测试集成到CI工作流中实现可重复评估、早期回归检测和整个软件开发生命周期的持续验证

Abstract: The increasing heterogeneity of high-performance computing (HPC) systems and the transition to exascale architectures require systematic and reproducible performance evaluation across diverse workloads. While continuous integration (CI) ensures functional correctness in software engineering, performance and energy efficiency in HPC are typically evaluated outside CI workflows, motivating continuous benchmarking (CB) as a complementary approach. Integrating benchmarking into CI workflows enables reproducible evaluation, early detection of regressions, and continuous validation throughout the software development lifecycle.
  We present exaCB, a framework for continuous benchmarking developed in the context of the JUPITER exascale system. exaCB enables application teams to integrate benchmarking into their workflows while supporting large-scale, system-wide studies through reusable CI/CD components, established harnesses, and a shared reporting protocol. The framework supports incremental adoption, allowing benchmarks to be onboarded easily and to evolve from basic runnability to more advanced instrumentation and reproducibility. The approach is demonstrated in JUREAP, the early-access program for JUPITER, where exaCB enabled continuous benchmarking of over 70 applications at varying maturity levels, supporting cross-application analysis, performance tracking, and energy-aware studies. These results illustrate the practicality using exaCB for continuous benchmarking for exascale HPC systems across large, diverse collections of scientific applications.

</details>
